###  Miete₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Miete* (though)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  48
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  LAST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
